MEDIAN - XL: ULTIMATIVE - XVI

General
  • Added over 150 endgame runewords. These are empowered versions of existing runewords. Any runeword based on Zod rune (or lower), can now be mixed with Xis rune for a level 120 version. For example: El-Xis on Helms will create level 120 Summit runeword.
  • Densities: reworked on all levels in order to achieve a better stability and performance, and make the difficulty curve more natural.
Uberquests/Monsters
  • Removed dumb 1HKO procs from several bosses.

  • The Void: fixed a bug that allowed boss seal to be destroyed by minions. Reworked boss fight.
  • Startled Witch: ensured no one will enter her grounds uninvited.
  • Uldyssian: final stage is now free-for-all. Modified Uldyssian AI. Stage #10 (totem) was reworked as it was buggy.
  • Kabraxis: now has a chance to teleport when struck to prevent lock abusing.
  • Athulua: slightly hardened.
  • MarcoNecroX: removed health regeneration and reduced damage. Just kidding. He now ignores immunity shields.

  • Baal (throne): no longer has a debuff aura on destruction.
  • Griswold: no longer has melee-only aura on terror / destruction.
Amazon
  • Increased cast rate with one handed weapons.
  • Thundercrack: fixed a (massive) bug that made lightnings not pierce.
  • Stormcall: increased damage.
  • Hammer of Zerae: incresed damage and weapon modifier from 3/4 to 3/2.
  • Magnetic Field: modified mechanics to work more efficiently, increased field density and max damage.
  • Pounce: slightly reduced range.
Assassin
  • Batstrike: fixed a bug that caused bats not getting any %avoid from Perfect Being. This means they were having effectively 1/10 as much survability as intended on the highest levels.
Druid
  • Now receives 25 health per level.
  • Werewolf Form: reworked attack rating formula.
  • Harbinger: fixed a bug that caused the skill not to check attack rating.
  • Elemental: now deals a reasonable amount of damage.

    • Yes, druid was a broken class. It was massively buffed some patches ago. Cry me a river.
Paladin
  • Dragon Oath: removed.
  • Dragonshout: removed.
  • Burnout: removed.
  • Demonrend: removed.
  • Deva King: removed.
  • Merkabah: removed.

  • New Skill: Solar Flare.
  • New Skill: Drakemaw.
  • New Skill: Frozen Breath.
  • New Skill: Incarnation.
  • New Skill: Dragon Wyrms.
  • New Skill: Dragonknight.

  • Superbeast: duration is now always 5 minutes.
  • Rapture: modified overlay.
  • Retaliate: adjusted damage to fit new skills.
  • Vessel of Retribution: adjusted damage values to have an effective damage similar to Vessel of Judgement.
  • Blessed Life: fixed a typo on the flat damage reduction formula (thanks @suchbalance).
  • Plague: is now a level 12 skill. Reworked damage formula, removed %block and added hard point synergy.
  • Dragonheart: renamed from Lionheart, no longer uses armor shrine overlay and no longer slows you down.
  • Hoplites: now have 50% physical resistance.
  • Tainted Blood: now adds 15% defense per hard point and 5% per soft point. Can no longer be casted on other players.
Sorceress
  • Leonardo: reduced knowledge. Less books in the air to prevent lag spikes.
  • Blade Spirits: now properly display hard point synergy.
  • Chronofield: now only affects running/walking speeds.
Oskills
  • Liche Form: reduced duration to 5 seconds.
  • Orb of Annihilation: can no longer be used on left-click.
  • Feral Strike: now works with swords instead of knives.
  • Ravage: now works with swords instead of knives.
  • Thorn Field: now works with swords instead of knives.
  • Shunpo: range increased by 25%.
Items
  • Giyua's Sacrum: now adds %fire spell damage instead of cold.
  • Hadriel Set: reworked to include cold spell damage and pierce.
  • The Grizzly (Secret): buffed stats. Big time..
  • Demonic Touch: replaced death projector reanimate with edyrem (works in toraja).
  • Reapers: renamed from Gehenna (helm). Removed Path of Flames oskill.
  • Segnitia: reduced flat damage to 100 and crushing blow to 5%.

  • Enchanting Crystals: items can now only be rolled once.
  • Elixirs: now last 30 seconds.
  • Jewels: can no longer be gambled.

  • I am Rich gem: color is no longer overriden by Ancient Repositories.
  • Character Orb: removed due to clunky mechanics, being unintuitive and having broken stat scaling.
Rare affix pool
  • Tantrum can now spawn in crossbows.
  • Bane can now spawn in sorceress orbs.
  • Terror Strike and Solar Flare can now spawn in paladin weapons.
Cube recipes
  • Removed athulua's blessing recipe.
  • Removed quest shortcuts that somehow never made it to the documentation.
Item drops
  • Certain bosses that had almost guaranteed chance to drop sacred uniques have been rebalanced.
  • Fixed a bug with shrine drops in The Void.
  • Griswold: now has 50% chance to drop special box in terror.
Bugfixes
  • Fixed Level Challenge 1 level requirement.
  • Fixed Athulua erroneously spawning in Tran Athulua.
  • Fixed gamebreaking state collision between Liche Form and Graveyard.
  • Fixed a bug that would allow people to use Yshari Set skills on regular areas.
  • Fixed a bug that allowed eagle stance to bypass immunity shields.
Other
  • Merkabah: removed.
  • NPC sell limits have been modified for acts 1 and 2 in hatred.
  • Cubing %experience orbs with weapons to make money is no longer a thing.
  • Shortened description of median statue because reading is too hard.
  • Removed unused assets in the patch to reduce size a bit.
  • Other minor bugfixes.
Special credits
  • suchbalance: general assistance and help creating new endgame runewords.
  • Inertia: skill icons and other assets.
 top

MEDIAN - XL: ULTIMATIVE - XVc

XVC BALANCE PATCH

New Uberquest: Zorun Tzin (Secret)
  • Replaces: Chrysaor (Secret Boss)
  • Reward: defeat Zorun Tzin on Destruction difficulty to get a skull of unknown power.
Uberquests
  • Athulua: fixed properties, no longer spawns from volcanic shrine, added improved death animation.
  • Uldyssian: fixed second stage.
  • World Nexus: increased Startled Witch's damage, increased mob density.
Amazon
  • Thundercrack: fixed description.
  • Hammer of Zerae: slightly increased lightning damage.
  • Asterism: increased stat bonuses.
  • Magnetic Field: increased lightning damage.
  • Lava Pit: increased damage.
  • Hyena Strike: %DR cap increased to 20%, base amount to 5%, fixed description.
Assassin
  • Backstab: removed timer, restricted to naginata, added duration progression with clvl, reduced attack rating, modified crushing blow formula.
Barbarian
  • Deathgaze: weapon damage is now 4/5 (you didn't see it coming), increased cold damage.
  • Daedalus: reduced softpoint based attack rating bonus per level from 10% to 5%.
Druid
  • Mana Pulse: fixed mana healed on description.
  • Feed the Pack: heal after kill now works only in wolf form.
  • Twisted Claw: removed NextDelay, now deals 3/5 weapon damage, slight mana increase.
Necromancer
  • Boneyard: slightly increased damage progression at early levels.
  • Funeral Pyre: increased minimum damage, reduced visual gfx, fixed synergy description.
  • Rotting Flesh: increased damage.
  • Pestilence: increased base damage and minimum damage per level.
Paladin
  • Hoplites: fixed max skill level description.
  • Scourges: fixed max skill level description.
Sorceress
  • Summon Blade Spirits: removed weapon requirement, fixed misplaced monprops.
Oskills
  • Raven Heart: now properly drains life.
Items
  • Str/Dex Damage Bonus: fixed on Cranebeak, Greil's Urvan, Forge Fire, Viperfork, Steel Pillar, Sky Scorcher, Divine Mandible, Tonbogiri, Polar Vortex, Wrath of Nature, Mistress of Pain, Glowing Vertigo & Tormentor.
  • Reaper's Hand: removed Queen of Blades oskill.
  • Periapt of Life UMO: now adds +100 replenish life.
  • Eye of Malic UMO: can now properly be cubed with quivers.
  • Sunstone of the Elements: fixed description.
  • Cornerstone of the World: removed Shadow Dancer & Life and Death cornerstones.
  • Mystical Blade: now drops again, fixed incompatibility issues with older patches.
  • Terror Box: can now spawn the new sets.
  • Ape Set: replaced +3 to All Skills with +18 to Deathstrike, and a few other changes to the set.
Other
  • Mystic Orbs: fixed many inconsistencies in the descriptions.
  • Scepters: fixed strength damage bonus appearing as a base affix.
  • Level Names: fixed a few inconsistencies with name colors. Act 5 uberquests are still white because... Blizzard.
  • Parrots: reverted velocity buff due to massive complaints.

MEDIAN - XL: ULTIMATIVE - XV

General

New Uberquest: Twin Seas
  • Replaces: Halls of the Dead Level 2.
  • Reward: defeat Athulua on Destruction difficulty to get Deity's Bow.
New Uberquest: World Nexus
  • Replaces: Flayer Dungeon Level 1, 2 & 3.
  • Reward: defeat the Startled Witch on Destruction difficulty to get The Sleep.
Uberquest Rework: The Unformed Land
  • Replaces: Sewers Level 1 & 2 (act 3).
  • Terul: name changed from Chrysaor, reworked skills.
  • Zorun Tzin (Secret Boss): name changed from Chrysaor (Secret).
Characters
  • New Characters: reduced the amount of initial items each character starts with. Use your gold!
  • Interface: overhauled skill tabs, isolating reward skills into an unique tab, and two tabs with 3 skill trees (15 skills) each.
  • Skills: updated build names/references on each skill tab's index, and improved GUI.
Uberquests
  • Yshari Sanctum: removed monster descriptions.
  • Rathma Square: removed flying scimitars.
  • Fauztinville: reduced UMO drop rate on hatred and terror.
  • Uldyssian: fixed most of the bugs when killing bosses on each stage.
Challenges
  • Level Challenge 1: replaced initial totem with a pirate, recipes overhaul:
    • Sunstone of the Elements + Sunstone of [...] ----> Sunstone of the Element with added bonuses
    • Maximum allowed level and swirlies are required just like before.
Monsters
  • MarcoNecroX (Secret Boss): improved sounds and graphics.
  • Brachyceran: his name no longer displays as FPBE string.
  • Pillar of Skulls: reduced Psychic Scream proc rate.
  • Blightfire: reduced health to prevent overflow.
  • Uldyssian: now has a chance to teleport away when struck.
Levels
  • Names: changed the name of some levels. Fixed the name of levels that had no level 2 variant (example: Stony Tomb).
  • Uberquest Warnings: removed and replaced with a red colored version of the level name, without 'To The'.
  • Halls of the Dead: now has a waypoint.
PlugY
  • Stat Summary: reworked & updated stat sheets. Added new stats. Improved layout.
  • Bugfix: fixed some stats displaying a maximum value of 63. To those who assume the stats were effectively capped at that number, l2p.

Amazon

Zerae's Devotion: Storm Askari
  • New Skill - Thundercrack: attack that channels lightnings to nearby enemies.
  • New Skill - Stormcall: call lightning to strike enemies within range.
  • New Skill - Hammer of Zerae: cast a spinning lightning enchanted mace dealing weapon damage.
  • New Skill - Asterism: passive, enhances your storm skills and increases defense.
  • New Skill - Magnetic Field: field of static lightning traps with rapidly fired shocks.
  • Sun Strike: improved skill description, changed gfx and skill icon.
  • War Spirit: changed skill icon.
  • Cast Rate: increased while wearing staves and other two-handed weapons.

    • Assasin

    Tree Rework: Claw
    • New Skill - Shadow Dancer: passive, increases damage while wielding two claws.
    • New Skill - Noctule: melee attack that spawns bats depending on enemies hit.
    Tree Rework: Ninja
    • New Skill - Backstab: powerful melee attack that renders you immune for a short time.
    • New Skill - Hades Gate: teleport into a corpse, damaging and knockbacking enemies.
    Tree Rework: Psychic
    • New Skill - Obliteration: field of concentrated energy that hits a huge amount of times.
    • Singularity: is now a level 18 skill.
    • Psionic Storm: changed skill icon. is now a level 12 skill.
    • Doom: now pierces 10% magic resistances as long as you invested hard points into the skill.
    Tree Rework: Martial
    • Way of the Spider: is now a level 6 skill.
    • Way of the Phoenix: is now a level 18 skill.
  • Cluster Mine: doubled base damage, slightly increased damage per level.
  • Tiefling Form: is now a level 24 skill. Added to states' morph group. This means it didnt collide with morphs before, and now will.

    • Barbarian

    Dualwielder Warrior
    • Blood Hatred: moved to new tree, is now a level 1 skill. Reworked mana and duration.
    • New Skill - Iron Spiral: create a fiery vortex of swords.
    • New Skill - Deathgaze: create a wild flurry of frozen axes.
    • New Skill - Daedalus: enhances barbarian's offensive capabilities.
    • New Skill - Windform: become the wind itself, spinning through enemies while greatly resisting damage.
  • New Skill - Iceburst: attack that creates an icy explosion through the ground.
  • Bear Stance: description now indicates that it only pierces physical resistances.
  • Stormblast: reverted graphics to pre-ultimative.
  • Titan Strike: increased duration.

    • Druid

    Shapeshifter: the Werewolf
    • New Skill - Werewolf Form: morph into a a vulnerable but deadly werewolf.
    • New Skill - Mana Pulse: melee attack that regenerates a flat amount of mana.
    • New Skill - Harbinger: warp into an :D causing all nearby :) to become :(.
    • New Skill - Feed the Pack: killed enemies can respawn as furious wolf allies.
    • New Skill - Twisted Claw: melee attack that creates a fast-hitting tornado.
  • Plague Avatar: greatly reduced lag.
  • Circle of Life: is now a level 18 skill to match the other passives.
  • Wildfire: moved to the 12-spot.
  • Mythal: changed skill icon.
  • Thorn Wall: increased damage from 3/4 to 5/4.

    • Necromancer

    Malice Wizard
    • New Skill - Boneyard: cast a ghost lance that does no damage but explodes on impact.
    • New Skill - Funeral Pyre: cast a horde of explosive zombies at target feet.
    • New Skill - Rotting Flesh: sacrifice a minion and use his remains to poison enemies.
    • New Skill - Nightwalker: passive, increases damage of malice spells and totem defense.
    • New Skill - Pestilence: cast a toxic storm that surrounds you for a short period.
  • Summon Veil King: dead veil king is now stronger. Just ensuring your irresponsible death.
  • Black Mass: mechanics rework to avoid cheesy stuff.
  • Fragmentation Shot: improved graphics.
  • Fireheart Totem: fixed description to mention reanimates.

    • Paladin

    Light's Influence
    • New Skill - Vessel of Retribution: rapidly casts short-ranged missiles to nearby enemies.
    • Rapture: changed speed's buff progression.
    • Solstice and Equinox: renamed from Light & Shadow, now affects Vessel of Retribution.
    • Sacred Armor: is now a Light Influence skill, changed skill icon.
    • New Skill - Hoplite: small group of highly damage resistant summons.
    Shadow's Influence
    • Vessel of Judgement: improved damage progression, minimum target count increased to 3.
    • New Skill - Euphoria: buff that decreases enemies' resistances.
    • New Skill - Life and Death: improves your Vessel of Judgement spell.
    • New Skill - Demiurge: become a devilish deity for a short period of time.
    • Scourges: is now a Shadow Influence skill.
    Dragonform Rework
    • Dragon Oath: fully reworked/improved mechanics, gfx, damage scaling, mana cost. Dragonform no longer locks other spells.
    • Dragonshout: tweaked damage, lowered NextDelay. Changed skill icon.
    • Burnout: slightly decreased max damage, reworked/improved mechanics and gfx, reduced lag as well and changed icon.
    • Demonrend: increased damage and changed skill icon.
    • Deva King: doesn't require killing a dragon anymore. Because people "were lazy".
  • Superbeast: added to states' morph group. This means it didnt collide with morphs before, and now will.
  • Tainted Blood: no longer mentions that it doesn't dispel superbeast.
  • Mind Flay: slightly reduced damage.

    • Sorceress

    Mana Tree
    • New Skill - Immersion: cast an arcane wave of mana to hurt enemies based on missing mana.
    • Mana Sweep: reduced NextDelay from 4 to 1.
    • Arcane Torrent: reduced mana cost so it synergically fits to the new skills, changed skill icon.
    • New Skill - Antimass: deplete all your mana and restore health based on the amount of mana consumed.
    Melee Tree
    • New Skill - Wraithsword: melee strike that deals damage based on nearby enemies.
    • New Skill - Fusillade: summon a deadly trap that shoots swords, killing everything in its way.
    • New Skill - Summon Blade Spirit: summon a group of allied swords that benefit from your passives.
    • Bladestorm: reduced weapon damage to 1/3, increased mana cost and capped conversion to 50%.
  • Symbol of Esu: reduced life healed per level from 400 to 200.
  • Flamestrike: changed gfx.
  • Abyss: slightly reduced damage to prevent cap overflow.
  • Thunderstone: slightly reduced damage.
  • Vengeful Power: fixed cap description.
  • Baneblade: reduced 20% damage per hard point to 10% (compensates for new skills).

    • Item-Only Skills

    Oskills
    • ATMG Sentry: reduced bonus duration per level from 0.4s to 0.2s.
    • Dual Veil King: deadly poison attack chance increased from 5% to 20%.
    • Jitan's Gate: now provides a short-lasting buff to you and allies after teleporting.
    • Time Freeze: reduced speed penalties to avoid crashes, duration increased to 0,2s.
    • Maelstrom: skill description now says it can be used with knives also.
    • Crane Stance: no longer affects allies, %avoid increased to 20% and damage per level from 15% to 20%.
    • Fowl Fight: skill description no longer mentions naginata requirement.
    • Porkulator: added to states' morph group. This means it didnt collide with morphs before, and now will.

    Items

    Sets:
    • New Set - Universal Law: assassin's psychic set.
    • New Set - Zerae's Divinity: amazon's storm set.
    • New Set - Tundra Walker: barbarian's dual axe set.
    • New Set - Marchosias' Essence: druid's werewolf set.
    • New Set - Celestial Orchard: necromancer's malice set.
    • New Set - Yaerius' Grey Omen: paladin neutral set. (no new sorceress set because she already has five)
    • Hadriel Set: removed dazzle bonuses, replaced with -50% EFR.
    • Imperius Set: now has Imperius reanimate again.
    • Malthael Set: now also adds poison pierce and spell damage.
    Unique Items:
    • New Item(s): added 30 Cornerstones of the World.
    • Cornerstone of the World: now has a note below the name indicating it cannot be unsocketed.
    • Dreadarc: fixed color collision on strings.
    • Steel Punisher: removed Deathlord morph.
    • Ballista: fixed fortress proc.
    • Forge Fire: fixed fortress proc.
    • Blackened: removed Duriel reanimate.
    Runewords:
    • Natasha's Legacy: increased base stats.
    • Eternal: fixed the (obviously) misplaced %damage stat and replaced with %ED.
    • Helgrotha: fixed bug that caused crash.
    • Lysra: fixed bug that caused crash.
    Uberquest Rewards:
    • Kabraxis' Stone: %max resistances are now rolled individually. Trinity Nova proc moved to base charm.
    • Class Charm: reorganized and improved stats display.
    • Book of Summoning: should now be cubed with Book of Lies instead of Astrogha's Venom Stinger.
    • The Sleep: removed str/dex bonuses from Tran Athulua trophy, now adds +200 magic damage and +50 damage reduction.
    • Cycles of Wisdom: fixed FPBE string error.
    Rare Affix Pool:
    • Indestructible: affix now spawns in the correct group.
    • Swords: now spawn with +druid skills.
    • Druid Staves: +(21 to 28) to Gamma Field
    • Scepters: wdm bonuses such as +min/max damage, %enhanced damage, etc. can now spawn.
    Miscellaneous:
    • Kabraxis' Stone: now has a note below the name indicating it cannot be unsocketed.
    • Elemental Runes: fixed black background color on DDraw mode.
    • Luck Trial Mystic Orb: can only be applied once.
    • Poison/Light Runes & Kabraxis' Stone: changed graphics.
    Base Items:
    • Scepters: are now properly considered maces (for runeword purposes).
    • Mammen Axe (2): now has 2 sockets.
    • Hexblade (2): now has 2 sockets.

    OTHER

    Miscellaneous
    • Interface: changed GUI as usual on all menus.
    • Mephisto Reanimate: after long sessions of therapy, he no longer commits suicide.
    • Champion of the Triune: fixed name.
    • Parrots: now fly 16% faster.

    Thanks for playing

  • Special Thanks to: Quirinus, manafire, Inertia, Nanashi, Necrolis & Alpha Team.

    MEDIAN - XL: ULTIMATIVE - XIV-b

    ▶ Bugfixes

    - Shrine Vessels: fixed bug when vessels had no charges.
    - Yshari Sanctum: fixed a bug where Seal of the Gods would have a delay or summon twice.
    - Force of Nature: fixed FPBE error.
    - Skill Signet: can no longer be eaten 4 times.
    - The Triune: fixed desync on Spire firecoils.
    - Spirit of Vengeance: fixed #1437 error.
    - Dark Summoning: fixed on hatred/terror.
    - Circle of Life: fixed.

    ▶ Assassin

    - Tiefling Form: fixed a bug that allowed ways to still do damage.
    - Tiefling Form: no longer adds +str, now gives +5 dexterity per level and +1 to all skills.
    - Tiefling Form: properly fixed attack/cast animations, attack animation is now slower and cast animation properly works with %FCR.

    ▶ The Void

    - Rathma & Mendeln: fixed bugged swirlies that wouldn't work all the time.
    - Rathma & Mendeln: fixed FPBE error when getting killed.
    - Rathma & Mendeln: reduced lag, fixed small bug in the summoning animation.
    - Mendeln: time freeze no longer affects hostile skeletons.
    - Walls now fade.
    - Darkness renamed to Darkspawn.
    - Eternals: slightly reduced drop rates.

    ▶ Uldyssian

    - Tomb guards can no longer be killed by charm.
    - Uldyssian's Sword: fixed FPBE.
    - Uldyssian's minions no longer bleed, to prevent lag.
    - Prime Edyrem #1: fixed health.
    - Prime Edyrem #5: slightly reduced health, lowered level of avalanche skill.
    - Fixed 8th wave.

    ▶ Other

    - Linarian's Legacy SU: finally fixed.
    - Triune walls now fade.
    - Swirlies: quests that use two type of them now use a different color for easier recognition.
    - Brachyceran's Lair: no longer drops ring of the five.
    - FullSet/Edyrem Aura: fixed buggy box and changed color again.
    - Devil's Fang Totem: fixed life amount to match the other totems.
    - Griswold: lowered difficulty on destruction, increased drops.

    top

    MEDIAN - XL: ULTIMATIVE - XIV

    ♦ Main Features

    - Uldyssian: completely redone uberquest! check it out if you want to have some fun.
    - New Item: Shrine Vessels - you can now store your shrines into a special vessel that holds up to 1000 shrines!

    ♦ Bugfixes

    - Entirely (hopefully) fixed #1437 error.
    - Fixed bug in Yshari Sanctum not allowing you to get full set.
    - Fixed bug that caused Baal to have only 1 hp in Destruction.
    - Fixed unsocket recipe for certain jewels.
    - Fixed Magineer reanimate string bug on Vizjun Set.
    - Fixed FPBE on The Void.
    - Fixed bug that caused Madawc/Korlic to not have %avoid. YOUMAD? - Talic. Reduced total %avoid on all.
    - Fixed Rathma's Chosen + Tainted Blood cheese. Ouch, cheesers.
    - Fixed a bug that caused elemental runes names not to appear when socketed.
    - Fixed bug that allowed uldyssian trophied to be cubed in The Sleep more than once. Refind it! (the charm)
    - Fixed a bug that caused some Yshari set pieces to drop from random superunique monsters.
    - Fixed a fixed fixed.

    ♦ Drop Rates

    - Tran Athulua: increased unique drop rates.
    - Bull Prince Rodeo: increased UMO drop chance from 1/50 to 1/30.
    - The Void: added NoDrop to eternals.

    ♦ Levels

    - Blood Moor: slightly reduced density.
    - Graveyard: modified map.
    - Duncraig: reverted to 1.Z9 map, added a new map variant.
    - Shadowgate Totems: lowered set drops a bit.

    ♦ Monsters

    - Griswold: slightly increased difficulty on terror/destruction.
    - Ennead Necromancer: now use Miasma, added small amount of %block.
    - MarcoNecroX Boss: reduced lags.

    ♦ Assassin

    - Tiefling Form: slightly increased cast speed, greatly increased attack speed. Shows skill timer.
    - Psionic Storm: slightly reduced mana cost.

    MXL: Ultimative X Released!

    MEDIAN XL: ULTIMATIVE X - CHANGELOG

    Main Features

    * New Uberlevel: The Triune (ACT 1 CATHEDRAL) - Difficulty: Very Hard.
    * New Itemtype: 'Cycles'. Can only be found in The Triune on destruction difficulty.
    * New Uberboss Experience: find the way and kill Arihan, High Priest of the Triune. The mechanics to do so are completely new!
    * New Quest Reward Charm: Kill Arihan and be rewarded with a Charm. If you're lucky, he will drop a Trophy, cube with it for extra bonuses.

    New Affix Groups (to reduce string overflow)

    * -# to Enemy Resistance bonuses will now stack if the values match. Does not include magic pierce, which is obsolete in MXL.
    * %IAS/FCR/FBR/FHR/FRW will now stack if the values match.

    Small Bugfixes / Tweaks

    * Chaos Reroll Recipe: ilvl of the output item reduced by 1%.
    * Kabraxis' Soul: due to a bug, removed elemental reanimates. The old charm is disabled. The new one contains:
    -- 50% Chance to Cast level 49 Trinity Nova on Death --
    * Kabraxis' Trophy: reduced reanimate chance to 2%.
    * Character Orb: fixed a bug that allowed you to use the charm at level 120. The old charm is disabled. You need to find a new one.
    * Bodysnatchers Runeword: now requires only 4 runes.
    * Shrinecrafting: fixed a few erroneous Shrine names.
    * Sinwar of the Storm: fixed a bug that caused him not to spawn in the Chaos Sanctuary.
    * Trap Rat: extended the health per level bonus to fit the new cap, allowing it to gain an extra of +1500 life instead of +300 (v7).
    * Skill Icons: fixed a few skill icons that were blinking random images when skilling.
    * If you are reading this, we agree that my english sucks.
    * Mystic Sword: fixed string, no longer displays as FPBE.
    * Blazing Fury: fixed duration.
    * MarcoNecroX Tribute Set: fixed buggy full set bonus colors.
    * Collosseum: fixed a bug in the description.
    * Fixed a bug that caused realm items to spawn in Single Player. I left this at the end because NOONE CARES.

    top

    Omega 003 -> 2012

    The Inferno rework

    Similar to Inferno difficulty in Diablo 3, the last difficulty is now the 'bonus difficulty' for maxed characters, instead of a stepping stone on your way to uberquests. This means it is much harder than before, but you can find sacred uniques and sets there now! The regular game, from level 1 to 120, is now compressed in only two difficulty levels, eliminating redundant redundancy and limiting the boredom of going through the whole godforsaken game 3 times before you can start farming.

    Destruction difficulty:
    - The hidden monster level 121 no longer exists, sacred uniques and sets drop off level 120 monsters as well.
    - Every monster in Destruction is level 120.
    - Monsters with a health multiplier below 300% were scaled up so the difference to 300% health is halved (for instance, a 100-120% Cursed Soul now has 200-210%, but a 285-370% Tenebral still has 285-370%).

    Terror difficulty:
    - Rescaled monster levels from 50 to 115, up from 50 to 90.
    - Increased Terror base monster stats.

    Experience gain:
    - Increased in Terror difficulty.
    - Greatly reduced experience gain past character level 115.

    General:
    - Monsters no longer move faster on higher difficulty levels.
    - Increased uberlevel monster health scaling to at least 1000% for most uberquests.

    The cold damage rework

    - Monster cold length is no longer reduced by difficulty level.
    - Every monster can now be chilled.
    - Cold chill now only slows by 20% against monsters.
    - Skill-based cold duration greatly increased.
    - Monsters now have a 25/50/75% chance to be immune to freeze.

    Characters

    - Reduced walk and run speed by 10%.
    - Changed barbarian, necromancer and sorceress select quote.
    - Corrected the listed damage on all weapon skills with added magic damage (thanks rad82).
    - Innate abilities now have a full description.
    - Minions now scale with clvl/2 instead of clvl*2 to prevent health overflow.
    - Reduced base block rates by 1% for all classes.

    Amazon

    - Wild and Free: reduced movement speed bonus by 5% at all levels.
    - Defensive Harmony: no longer slows enemies that swing at you and miss.

    - Wyrmshot: submissiles are now fire arrows instead of fire swords (?!).

    - Pounce: uses a different way to calculate flat damage to prevent overflow at high stat/skill levels.

    - Moonbeam: fixed graphic.

    - Blood Elementals: corrected damage display.

    Assassin

    - Storm Crows: corrected damage description (you were hoping for a buff right?) xD
    - Maelstrom MkIV: developed in secret to skirt the ban on fragmentation weapons, the 'Scylla' upgrade features flechettes magnetically coated in monomolecular flecks of metal stripped from the user's weapons, which seems to trigger the wapons' magical enchantments on impact. This technology rendered the projectile too bulky to pierce through enemies, but with this design requirement out of the way, space was found for a heavier fuel-air warhead to deal with immune targets, giving the wielder two effective forms of attack.

    - Batstrike: corrected bat familiar damage display.
    - Barrier Strike: base crit chance is now 5% as displayed, not 0%; increased blade duration to 2.4 seconds.
    - Twin Fang Strike: removed annoying sound effect.

    - Limpet Laser replaces Cryo Beam: sticky grenade that is thrown against a wall and fires cryo beams at nearby enemies.

    - Way of the Phoenix: reduced base damage to 15-20 from 20-35.
    - Way of the Gryphon: reduced base damage to 1-40 from 1-50.

    - Blink: correctly displays stun length again.
    - Perfect Being: reduced EHP% per level from 6-5-4-3-2 to 5-4-3-2-2.

    - Bionetic Blast: now causes knockback (1/3) instead of stagger; increased aoe radius by 20%.
    - Psionis Storm: increased radius; targets close to the middle are now staggered.
    - Beacon: doubled fire damage and massively increased physical damage.

    Barbarian

    - Corrected minion life display (looks like a big nerf, but it's just the skill display matching up with actual life now) (*)

    - Titan Strike: now starts at 10% armor instead of 0%.

    - Snake Stance: slow target caps at 35%, down from 50%.
    - Bear Stance: reduced armor to 10% per level, down from 15%.

    - Wolf Companion: Doom radius is no longer bugged; no longer die to reflected damage; halved Doom damage.
    - Fortress: increased timer to 7-3 seconds from 5-2 seconds, increased rate of fire from 15 frames to 10 frames.

    - Shamanic Trance: reduced life bonus due to overflow.

    (*) Thanks rad82. May be off by 2 life because I'm too lazy to do it properly. Hard math is hard.

    Druid

    - Blindside: now costs 0 mana.
    - Cascade: halved mana cost.
    - Elfin Arrows: increased base DS from 5% to 15%.
    - Nova Shot: increased magic damage bonus per arrow.

    - Freezing Gale: slightly increased damage per second.

    - Treewarden Form: now slows 50% up from 25%.
    - Pummel: now correctly uses attack rating.

    Necromancer

    - Voodoo Shot (renamed from Widowmaker) now gains +1 missile per soft point; added a graphic to indicate origin area.

    - Summon Shadows: reduced Demon Blood elemental damage bonus from 7% per level to 4%.

    - Rathma's Chosen: now has 1/8 chance to play a new sound.
    - Graveyard: new cast sound.

    - Frostclaw Totem: increased collision size (preventing misses)
    - Fireheart Totem: doubled rate of fire, reduced targets from 4 to 2, increased splash damage radius.

    Paladin

    - Plague is now the holy uberskill, and Resurrect is now the neutral uberskill.

    - Retaliate: now has only 66% chance to knockback, down from 100%.
    - Merkabah: replaced sound effects (thanks Arthandas).
    - Colosseum: replaced sound effects (thanks Arthandas); no longer requires a melee weapon.

    Morninglord rework:
    - New skill: Sunstorm (replaces Glittering Regalia): channel to shoot a stream of glowing bolts at the nearest enemy, doing tons of damage.
    - Brimstone: now a delayed detonation instead of a trap.
    - Ring of Light, Brimstone and Rising Dawn now grant you the 'Resonance' buff (+50% total defense and 1/2 energy added to strength) if you are in a specific spot to absorb the spell's energy.
    >>> Resonance bonus to Searing Glow: +3 second dazzle duration.
    >>> Resonance bonus to Sunstorm: now hits all nearby enemies.

    - Vessel of Judgement: reduced lightning sound volume.

    Sorceress

    - Ice Elementals: corrected damage and attack rating display.
    - Snow Queen: increased life bonus cap from 25% to 30%.

    - Firedance: timer now starts at 5 seconds and decreases to 0; no longer adds 25% IAS, but instead adds 50% ED +2% per soft point.
    - Miasma: slightly reduced damage and attack rating penalties to enemies.

    Other skills

    - Fixed erroneous scaling of a number of non-learnable summoning skills.
    - Fixed the damage and attack rating display of a number of non-learnable summoning skills (not a stat nerf).

    - New skill: Shunpo (assassin naginata oskill): essentially a Pounce clone with reduced AoE and no timer.

    - Claw Tornado: ND reduced to 4, now deals 3/4 damage and always shoots 5 tornadoes.
    - Dark Summoning: has a 10 second cooldown again. Stop cheesing!
    - Detonate: now always deals 5K physical damage to the target; it is no longer dependent on energy.
    - Fear Bomb Totem: no longer gains an undocumented HP bonus from Stormeye Totem.
    - Hammertime: all sources of this now always produce 10 hammers.
    - MIRV: now correctly uses Beacon scaling.
    - Pandemonium: added Fallen Sarandesh and Mahasattva to the monster pool.
    - Shadow Blade: fixed error that resulted in the wrong (annoying) sound being played (over and over and over).
    - Summon Daystar: spell damage bonus per level reduced from 10% to 5%.
    - Summon Edyrem: life no longer erroneously scales with character level, but now has 75% chance to avoid damage.
    - Zen Bolt: fixed graphic.

    The Slow change

    The Slow Target modifier on (most) off-weapon items and socketables is now Slow Melee Target, which slows your target on attack. If you have a source of regular slow, the regular slow will overwrite it as soon as the attack actually lands. If you do not, your direct target is now severely slowed.

    Fixed issue that caused the slow modifier to spawn both slow and melee slow.

    This impacts existing items as following (only includes items where the slow was changed and nothing else, otherwise see the items section of the changelog):

    Items that were changed to Slow Melee Target

    * Runewords:
    - Snowsquall

    * Uniques (existing instances get a required level of 555 and become unusable):
    - Grimspirit
    - Oreichalcos
    - The Gauntlet
    - Xepera Xeper Xeperu

    * Crafts:
    - Slow crafted jewels

    Items that automatically update
    No action is necessary.

    * Runewords (containing Zod):
    - Gharaniq: 5% slow -> 5% melee slow.

    * Socketables:
    - Zod runes: 5% slow -> 5% melee slow.

    Items that were not changed

    * Every weapon unless mentioned elsewhere.

    * Runewords:
    - Amaymon

    * Uniques:
    - Deadman's Hand
    - The Sightless Eye

    * Sets:
    - Full set: Caoi Dulra.
    - Full set: Cinadide's Craft.

    Slow removed entirely
    See below under the 'items' section because this is technically an item rebalance, not a slow modification.

    - Creature of Flame: remake. He kills players instantly with physical damage. However, he is surrounded by Astral Guardians whose attack phases players, granting them immunity to physical damage.

    1.Z9 -> Omega

    Characters

    - Skill-based animation speed bonuses reduced because skill IAS is WAY more powerful than item IAS and made it very easy to reach max speed.
    - Energy bonus display on spells now correctly counts strength factor as well.
    - 'Slow' is now dispelled when the monster is struck by an attack.
    - Reworded many spell descriptions of abilities based on base stats, replacing the 'per 100 [stat]' with 'percent of [stat]'.

    Amazon

    - Bloodlust: description is now more verbose.

    - Ghost Arrow: now gains an extra arrow every 7 levels, up from 10.
    - Barrage: duration fixed at 1 second, but now shoots 45 arrows during this time, each with bonus magic damage; increased mana cost.
    - Phalanx: slightly increased wall length; added 10% chance to knockback.
    - Dragonlore (renamed from Trinity): increased self-synergy from 10% to 15%.
    - Wyrmshot (renamed from Dragonforce): reduced attack rate from 1 shot every 12 frames to 1 shot every 13 frames (not less damage, but more spacing between shots, extending range but potentially reducing concentrated dps).

    - Moonbeam: improved graphics.
    - Ricochet: increased base number of hits from 3 to 5; increased range; reduced mana cost; +2 targets per skill level, up from +1.
    - Moon Queen: reduced IAS bonus; added deadly strike bonus based on hard points; life per kill is now soft point based.
    - Fairy Ring: added 1 second timer.

    - Magic Missiles: reduced cast sound volume; removed bounce sound; missiles per level is now linear.
    - Balefire: corrected bug that caused the afterflames to deal 1/4 damage (whoops); increased mana cost; afterflame duration reduced at low levels, but now increases with level.
    - Bloodstorm: reduced missile speed; duration now matches description (+0.2 seconds per level down from +0.4); damage slightly increased; seek range no longer increases with level, increasing accuracy against nearby targets.

    - Takedown (renamed from Triumphant Strike): reduced IAS bonus. ^
    - Lioness: slightly increased defense per level.

    - Balance: added a self-synergy to improve the defense bonus.
    - Defensive Harmony: clarified effect.

    - Curare: reduced poison length.
    - Spellbind: greatly increased duration at higher levels; increased range by 25%.
    - War Spirit: new cast sound.

    Assassin

    - Added timer reduction per hard point to Blink, Singularity and Vampiric Icon.

    - New innate skill - Bloodbath: dual claw attack that provides a buff that grants life per kill and claw block based on dexterity.
    - New skill - Barrier Strike (replaces Hades Gate): melee attack that creates a blade circle that repels enemies outside the radius, damaging them.
    - New skill - Twin Fang Strike (replaces Black Lotus Strike): a melee attack that deals area effect fire and poison damage.
    - New skill - Laserblade (replaces Death Blossom): passively adds damage to naginata area effects.
    - New skill - Cluster Mine (replaces Seal of Fire): creates a carpet of landmines.
    - New skill - Bionetic Blast (replaces Premeditation): deals physical damage and stagger at target point, damage based on energy.
    - New skill - Psychic Scream (replaces Way of the Raven): area effect fear around caster.

    - Upgraded skill - Electrofield Sentry: the official Raven Ops spec update of the M-520 'Storm Cloud' Portable Point Defense Sentry replaces the unsubtle chain lightning with a small scale electric discharge for stealth purposes while enhancing the power of the final nova explosion. Time until detonation is currently fixed at 2 seconds, but a future upgrade will allow operatives to detonate the sentry remotely.

    - Way of the Spider: reduced low level damage, increased damage ramp at high levels.
    - Doom: the damage synergy is now a self-synergy.

    - Cryo Beam: reduced freeze length, replaced knockback with a stagger effect; increased damage, reduced sound volume.

    - Storm Crows: now fires +1 extra knife per level after killing an enemy; removed bounce sound.
    - Maelstrom: due to the recent treaty restricting the manufacture and use of fragmentation weapons, the Maelstrom system was redesigned to minimise civilian casualties while concentrating more damage on the intended targets. The RPS-8 'Maelstrom MkIII' rocket-propelled flechette dispenser has a bigger blast radius on a direct hit and submissile damage is now based on the user's dexterity, preventing on-striking procs from going off in unintended directions and causing collateral damage. To compensate for the loss of damage, the flechettes are now fired in a spiral trajectory for improved short range coverage.
    - Broadside: improved graphics by adding a device that shoots the knives.

    - Perfect Being: rebalanced avoidance %: now it gives +10% 'effective HP' (ie. damage to death) +6% to +2% per level at a linear rate. Even though the avoidance percentage slows down as it approaches 100%, you continue getting 6-2% survivability for every point.

    - Beacon: new cast sound; now adds 1% movement speed per soft point when active; damage is now fixed (except for items); delay before call-in reduced from 170 frames to 85.

    Barbarian

    - Titan Strike: description is now more verbose.

    - New skill - Nephalem Weapons: enchants the weapons of the party with elemental damage based on your stats.

    - Bloodhatred: corrected description.
    - Thunder Slam: added flat magic damage per base strength, but fixed radius.

    - Bear Claw: removed annoying sound effect.
    - Screaming Eagle: enemy damage reduction now caps at -25%.
    - Overkill: reduced impact scatter radius to improve density and increase damage; removed graphics and sound.

    - Ancient Blood: reduced IAS bonus.
    - Fortress: timer now reduced with hard points, down to 2 seconds; corrected description to reflect this is spell lockout and not a timer.
    - Spirit Guide: now gives the correct amount of ED%.
    - Spirit Walk: removed sound.

    - Lion Stance.
    - Snake Stance: slow capped at 50%.
    - Eagle Stance: rebalanced heal rate.
    - Wolf Stance: reduced IAS bonus; movement speed bonus is now linear, but caps at +120%.

    Druid

    - Mark of the Wild: description is now more verbose; now has the correct duration.
    - Goodberries can now be duplicated in the cube (1 > 3) like symbols of Esu.

    - New skill: Idol of Scosglen (replaces Rampage): turns you into stone for 4 seconds increasing defense, after which you shatter, stunning enemies.
    - New skill: Mythal (replaces Gamma Field): creates a field of wild magic that reduces enemy resistances.
    - New skill: Elvensong (replaces Charm): summons a fey that attempts to charm enemies; has 50/70/90% avoid.

    - Cascade: restricted arrow range, but allowed seek range to go up all the way to the chunk edge (to enable multihits at close range).
    - Nova Shot: range now starts low and scales up.

    - Elemental: simplified graphics to reduce sprite load.
    - Hunting Banshee: removed annoying scream sound.
    - Freezing Gale: new icon.

    - Poison Flash: removed poison length increase per level; improved poison length synergy; improved minimum damage; improved flee synergy; added slow thorns while casting.
    - Plague Avatar: changed cast sound.
    - Acid Fiends: increased poison flash self-synergy from 40% to 60%. Did you know this actually inherits your +% poison spell damage and -% poison resist? Also renamed aura to Venomous Aura and removed transparency. Text for the text wall! Changes for the change log!

    - Pummel: increased area of effect.
    - Wildfire: damage now based on strength instead of energy.
    - Circle of Life: increased self-synergy from 15% to 25% and improved heal ramp.

    - Trap Rat Form: increased defense from 5% per level to 10% per level.
    - Quill Storm: reduced missile count to 15 per target, but increased damage to 2/3 weapon damage and added flat magic damage.
    - Egg Trap: reduced damage from 3/4 to 3/5, but reduced delay between spike novas to ensure more hits on individual targets.
    - Thorn Wall: wall pieces now break down when touched, but deal 1/2 damage up from 1/4.

    Necromancer

    - New skill: Burning Veil (replaces Unholy Armor): wall that invokes bloodlust in allies passing through it.

    - New skill: Bane (replaces Oathbreaker Totem): enemies around target minion are cursed with amplify damage.
    - New skill: Graveyard (replaces Liche Form): periodically shoots a punisher at a nearby enemy.

    - Summon Rampagor: no longer transparent; increased poison damage per second and length.
    - Summon Veil King: reduced damage to prevent overflow.
    - Summon Void Archon: reduced damage to prevent overflow.

    - Parasite: +2 targets per skill level, up from +1.

    - Widowmaker: now lasts 0.8 seconds and fires 24 arrows, but now also adds a +base weapon damage bonus (experimental). This spell was balanced, so I regret having to do this, but the 'trap' effect (the emitter stays in place) was stupid.

    - Bend the Shadows: no longer has a skill timer, but now inflicts a phase curse on you, duration reduced at higher levels.
    - Talon's Hold: now gives some slow from soft points, but also +1% per hard point.

    - Frostclaw Totem: modified mechanics to reduce lag and increases damage consistency.
    - Fireheart Totem: instead of a stream of firebolts, now fires Flamefront bolts with splash damage; narrowed damage variance to prevent damage overflow.
    - Stormeye Totem: increased rate of fire but reduced maximum number of lightning bolts and damage.

    - Black Mass: increased radius.
    - Rathma's Chosen: randomised sound effect.

    Paladin

    - Vindicate: description is now more verbose; improved graphics.

    - New skill: Colosseum (displaces Blessed Life): jump into an enemy and raise an arena, inside which the enemies are weakened; enemies outside are knocked back.
    - New skill: Glittering Regalia (replaces Wrath): increases spell damage based on gold carried.
    - New skill: Symphony of Destruction (replaces Punisher): periodically explodifies a nearby enemy with the power of awesome.

    - Blessed Life is now a level 90 skill (replaces Sovereignty).
    - Blessed Life: now gains 2% DR per level, up from 1%; greatly increased flat damage reduction bonus; increased potion heal rate bonus.

    - Hammerstrike: now deals 3/2 weapon damage; increased nova radius.
    - Merkabah: now an explosion effect to avoid ND issues; this necessitated a few other changes - no longer deals weapon damage or increases in radius per level, but does magic damage equal to 25% of base strength per skill level; now has a 4% chance per hard point to deal x4 damage.
    - Lionheart: now also has a max level synergy from Hammerstrike and Colosseum; increased defense bonus; now adds a static 25% of strength to vitality when active.
    - Searing Glow: removed physical damage, but added a dazzle component that sets enemy attack rating to 0 for a while.

    - Swapped Black Sleep and Lemures in the skill tree.
    - Terror Strike: increased base defense bonus.
    - Black Sleep: reduced duration (this is a buff).
    - Blood Thorns: slightly increased damage.
    - Hymn: now has increasing returns instead of diminishing returns (major buff); duration is now affected by a Terror Strike synergy.
    - Tainted Blood: greatly increased duration, added 5% defense per point.
    - Slayer: increased number of shots from 10 to 15.
    - Stormlord (renamed from Dark King): improved synergy from 4% to 7%. The weather for today: stormy with a chance of METAL.

    - Vessel of Judgement: slightly increased damage; now has correct damage progression; no longer affected by attack rating and just always hits; duration greatly increased.
    - Rapture: removed timer and increased duration based on hard points, but reduced effect; movement speed is now linear; removed sound.

    - New skill: Vengeful Power (displaces Lorenado): passive, increases life and grants a damage boost when struck.

    ** Now targets an area and deals poison damage.

    - Nova Charge: now adds 15% of your base dexterity to energy when cast.

    - Arcane Torrent: reworked damage formula; added a physical component based on current mana; halved range; changed sound effect.
    - Mana Sweep: reworked damage formula; now steals a fixed amount of mana per target.

    ** Duration extended.

    Cube recipes

    - New! Item Destruction recipe: just about any item + Catalyst of Destruction -> Catalyst of Destruction. Too many items cluttering your inventory and the floor? Problem solved!
    - New! RIP recipe: any wearable item + Catalyst of Destruction + Arcane Crystal -> adds RIP to item. If you've gone wild with reanimates and can't see the forest for the treewardens, this solves it.

    - To improve discoverability and simplify the cube recipes, there are 7 new consumable reagents ('oils') and 3 new reusable reagents ('catalysts') which can be bought for cheap at your local armor vendor. The corresponding recipes have been modified:
    Dupe recipe (item + Oil of Duplication + arcane crystal)
    Unsocket recipe (item + Oil of Disjunction; if nonmagical, you still need 3 perfect gems)
    Quality upgrade recipe (several, see docs)
    Chaos reroll recipe (item + Oil of Luck + jewel)
    Lucky upgrade recipe (item + Oil of Luck)
    Jewelcrafting (jewel + Oil of Jewelcrafting + appropriate rune)
    Respec (Oil of Absolution + rune)

    Disenchant recipe (unique/set item + Catalyst of Disenchantment)
    Signet recipe (unique/set item + Catalyst of Learning)
    Affix burn recipe (item + Catalyst of Destruction + rune)

    - Expanded the disenchant and signet recipes:
    Disenchant recipe: can now also disenchant set items for 1 shard.
    Signet recipe: reduced to 1 signet (due to Dat Bug), but can now also disenchant unique items for 1 signet.

    - Dupe recipe: can now dupe every wearable item, however it will add a +5 required level penalty to both duped items if the items are not jewels. Also, it cannot dupe already duped items, again if the items are not jewels.
    - Unique uptier recipe: now requires a rune instead of a gem.
    - Zomghelp recipe: now requires a magic amulet and ring instead of a rare one.

    - I Am Rich recipe: now requires three precious trophies, but the resulting gem now causes you to emit a red halo that is visible to you and most importantly everyone else. Earlier versions of this item now say 'Poser!'.

    Levels

    - The following dungeons are now level 121 on Destruction difficulty and can therefore drop sacred uniques and sets:
    -- Act 3 Durance of Hate Level 3.
    -- Act 4 Chaos Sanctuary.
    -- Act 5 Throne Room and Worldstone Keep.
    Beware, this also means the monsters are harder!

    Heroics

    - Greatly reduced the size of the Stony Tomb Level 1 heroic level; increased Quov Tsin chance accordingly.
    - Improved drop quality of heroic level monsters.

    - Bull Prince Rodeo: Hoof Stomp now ignores defense; his normal attack now knocks back.

    Challenges

    - Veteran Challenge
    Near the end of each Act in Terror and Destruction difficulty, you may randomly find a group of special monsters. Kill them in Terror and they will drop exactly one token. Cube all tokens with your class charm to get a bonus.

    - Slayer Challenge
    Kill Act bosses in Terror or Destruction. They will drop a token in addition to their regular drop. Cube all tokens, but include one of the Prime Evil tokens 3 times (eg. Andariel, Duriel, Mephisto/Mephisto/Mephisto, Diablo, Baal) to

    get a Signet of Skill.

    - Level Challenge 2
    Simply kill Primus (Rathma Square) in Terror difficulty and cube your class charm with a perfect gem for a bonus. Also, you need to do this before level 90.

    - To make the Black Road Challenge (BRC) viable in Terror difficulty, King Koth, Tran Athulua and Fauztinville are now level 80 in Terror, down from 90-105. Additionally, Tran Athulua and Fauztinville monsters have the same stat% in Terror as in Hatred instead of boosted stats.

    - To make the Level Challenge 2 viable in Terror difficulty, the Rathma Square uberlevel is now level 80 in Terror, down from 95 and you gain no experience there in Terror.

    Minigames
    Newly introduced in 1.E9, these are a collection of 'tasks' that result in a max skill level bonus.

    - Witch Blood
    Find the Countess in Terror difficulty. Kill her and cube your charm with an Eth rune (r05) for a bonus. By the way... the Countess dungeon's inhabitants are a bit unusual this time round.

    - Crowned
    Witches appear in specific areas and do not want to be disturbed. If you come too close, you are in trouble. This minigame is active on Terror difficulty and requires you to find a witch in any Act except Act 1. (This will
    not work on Act 1 witches). SLOWLY creep closer and see if a glowing star appears on your character. If so, cube your class charm with a Thul rune (r10). But be careful: too close and you're witch food.

    - They Have Windows In Hell
    In Act 4, you can find stained glass windows. Break one of these windows on Terror or Destruction difficulty and cube your class charm with a Hel rune (r15) while affected by the swirl effect to get a bonus.

    - Mirror Mirror
    In Act 5 Terror or Destruction difficulty, go to the final fight with Baal and kill his shardspawn minions. Only his minions! An average of 250 kills later, you will get swirlies. Cube your class charm with a Lem rune (r20)
    for a bonus.

    Uberquests

    - Added a high chance to avoid damage and poison length reduction in Destruction difficulty to the following bosses:
    -- Tal Rasha
    -- King Koth
    -- Akarat
    -- Avatar of Zakarum
    -- Bull Prince Rodeo
    -- Belial
    -- Quov Tsin
    -- Astrogha

    - Duncraig: massively increased Sacred drop rate (x4 when an item is rolled)

    Drop rates

    - All Act bosses and Nihlathak should now drop only uniques and runes.

    - Enabled Signets of Greater Gold, Greater Experience and Learning to drop.
    Low level monsters: 66% Gold, 33% Experience.
    High level monsters: 50% Gold, 25% Experience, 10% Greater Gold, 10% Greater Experience, 5% Learning.

    - The Smith has a signet drop bias.
    - Nihlathak has 50% chance to drop a Signet of Learning in Hatred, always drops one in Terror and drops 3 in Destruction.

    Misc

    - Greatly reduced cost of mystic orbs.
    - Greatly reduced cost of reagents. (OMG something in the game costs money, the horror!)
    - Increased the power of experience signets.
    - Reduced experience gain after level 116.

    - Book of Summoning is now 1x1.

    - Reduced the speed of the Punisher Nova trap.

    1.D9c -> 1.E9 RC

    Changes in the RC marked in yellow.

    Characters

    - New block paradigm: all shields have 0% block; class-specific shields have 1% block. However, characters have an innate block rate: amazon, assassin, sorceress = 4%; druid: 3%; paladin, necromancer: 2%; barbarian: 1%. Also, Lionheart and Baneblade give +1% block, and Trap Rat Form gives +4%.
    The following skills can now be mapped under the left click:
    - Bloodlust
    - Blood Elementals
    - Wolf Companion
    - Acid Fiends
    - All necromancer summons
    - Merkabah
    - Shadowfiends
    - Vessel of Judgement
    - Rapture
    - Ice Elementals
    - Faerie Fire
    - Tremor
    - Baneblade
    - Scourge
    - War Spirit
    - Thundergod
    - Golden Calf

    Amazon

    - Bacchanalia: maximum damage is now attained earlier, but is lower.

    Assassin

    - Starburst: now correctly uses +% physical/magic spell damage.

    Barbarian

    - Melee combat skills now work only with a strength-based weapon.
    - Undid the above.
    - Titan Strike: now grants 10% defense per level.
    - Undid the above due to negative feedback.
    - Shower of Rocks: added -25% enemy attack speed debuff.
    - Stormblast: now 3/4 damage.
    - Lion Stance: extra damage penalty reduced to 25% from 50%.

    Druid

    - Elfin Weapons: corrected description.

    Necromancer

    - Widowmaker: damage increased from 1/3 to 2/3.
    - Unholy Prayer: now a left click skill.

    Paladin

    - Melee combat skills now work only with a sword, blunt weapon or spear, excluding javelins and daggers.
    - Undid the above.

    Sorceress

    - Ice Elementals: added 25% damage reduction to their Frost Armor aura.
    - Lightning Cascade: slightly reduced maximum damage.
    - Lorenado: increased maximum damage.

    Others

    - Glacial Nova: rebalanced freeze time: shorter at low level, then increases.
    - Shadow Blade: removed timer, increased minimum damage, added stun.

    Items

    Base items

    - Added 'Amazing Grace' property to paladin spears: 5% chance to become immune for 1.2 seconds on attack.
    - Amazing Grace now has a graphic.
    - Reduced damage of sacred warp blades and all sceptre types.
    - Reduced attack rate of all sceptre types.
    - Increased attack rate of war sceptres again.
    - Improved warp blade damage again.
    - Increased damage and attack rate of necromancer scythes.

    +% bonus to an attribute
    +maximum damage

    - Soulshatter oskill added to scythes.

    Cube recipes

    top

    1.A9c -> 1.D9

    Characters

    - Damage synergies completely removed. This is compensated by the energy buff below.
    - Diminishing returns curve on spell damage is much flatter, avoiding the discouraging 1/4 at high skill levels.
    - Energy bonus to spell damage has a flatter curve, meaning more damage at higher energy values.
    - Mana costs now increase at 50% their previous rate.
    - Reduced inert duration of sacrifice effects.
    - Greatly increased cast speed of sorcs and druids with staves and attack speed of barbs with 2h weapons.

    Amazon

    - Dragon Lady
    Dragonforce: reduced submissile rate, but increased damage to match.

    - Moonfury
    Moonbeam: added magic damage conversion.
    Ricochet: added cold damage conversion; reduced bounces.
    Enfilade: added magic damage conversion.
    Moon Warrior: added life per kill.
    Fairy Ring: added fire damage conversion.

    - Bloodwitch
    Magic Missiles: now a level 1 skill, damage adjusted accordingly.
    Bloodstorm: increased damage.
    Lava Pit is a new level 24 skill, replacing Death Ray.

    - Huntress

    Pounce: radius locked, but gains damage from str or dex.
    Great Hunt: increased damage; changed graphics.

    - Spirit of Vengeance: uses a more intelligent AI that follows the player; changed cast sound; is now invulnerable!
    - War Spirit: now hits every 2 seconds instead of every second, but does double damage.

    Assassin

    - Batstrike: increased AR, greatly increased charge duration; bats now inherit PB.
    - Crucify: may now shoot up to 8 extra missiles depending on nearby enemies.
    - Queen of Blades: changed cast sound.

    - Way of the Spider: rebalanced damage progression.

    - Cryo Beam is a new level 6 skill, replacing Rune of Ice.
    - Immolation Bomb: corrected damage progression.

    - Psionic Storm is a new level 18 skill, replacing Rain of Bombs.

    - Storm Crows: increased damage.
    - Wychwind: reduced timer.
    - Maelstrom Mk.II is a new level 18 skill, replacing Rocket Blade.

    - Beacon: changed cast sound.
    - Way of the Gryphon: doubled damage.
    - Way of the Raven: increased damage.

    Barbarian

    - Fortress: reduced starting timer and improved timer progression.
    - Spirit Guide: aura refreshes faster; radius increased; missing FCR bonus added to description.

    - Titan Strike: colourshift should now override armour colours.

    - Increased run speed of spirits.
    - Spirit Walk is a new level 24 skill, replacing Shaman's Path.
    - Protector Spirit: now gets a lot of Bloodlust damage from level.

    - Rebound: reduced axes per level; reduced damage.
    - Screaming Eagle: now also slows the targets; increased radius.
    - Overkill is a new level 24 skill, replacing Hawk Talons.

    - Snake Stance: rebalanced damage progression.

    - Wolf Stance: CB is now a self-synergy.
    - Shamanic Trance: improved graphics; now offers str-based bonuses to minions; now adds +1 spirit per hard point.

    Druid

    - Elfin Arrows: desc now reflects that it also affects forms.
    - Spore Shot: now 3/4 damage.
    - Nova Shot: now 3/4 damage.

    - Removed both charm trees, eliminating the unpopular charm druid build in favour of two shapeshifting trees.
    - The new Trap Rat tree:
    Trap Rat Form
    Quill Storm
    Egg Trap
    Ferocity
    Thorn Wall
    - The new Treewarden tree:
    Treewarden form
    Pummel
    Circle of Life (moved from the poison tree)
    Wildfire
    Rampage

    - Charm: takes the place of Circle of Life in the poison tree.
    - Pagan Rites: now castable under skill lockout.

    - Hailstorm: improved graphics by removing bugged light radius.
    - Rain of Fire is a new level 18 skill, replacing Fire Fountain.

    - Poison Flash: increased duration.
    - Acid Fiends: fixed desc.

    - Force of Nature: increased bonus.
    - Goodberry: recipe now works only with druids.

    - Mark of the Wild is now an innate skill; you get it in your icon list for free.

    Necromancer

    - Minion tree overhaul:
    Summon Darklings removed.
    Summon Rampagor and Summon Lamia moved up.
    Summon Veil King is a new level 18 skill.

    - Combat tree overhaul:
    Soulshatter and Deathstrike removed.
    Massacre is a new level 18 skill.
    Deathlord is a new level 24 skill.

    - Totem trees overhaul:
    Exploding Totem and Totemic Mastery removed.
    Frostclaw Totem moved up to level 1.
    Totembound Guardians is a new level 6 skill.
    Oathbreaker Totem is a new level 18 skill.

    - Famine: increased damage bonus.
    - Buckshot: uses a new skill function to remove the need to click at the edge of the screen to get a focussed blast.

    - Summon Jinn: Hellfire Aura radius increased.

    Paladin

    - Retaliate: radius locked, but now gains damage per strength.
    - Hammerstrike is a new level 6 skill, replacing Holy Insanity.
    - Merkabah: renamed from Edict of Forbiddance, and now also deals fire damage and converts damage to fire damage; radius locked, but now gains damage per strength.

    - Searing Light: added physical damage component.
    - Brimstone is a new level 12 skill, replacing Holy Trap.

    - Shadowfiends: now also inherit Plague.

    - Tainted Blood: now heals faster for each additional point spent, but is now hard pooint based.
    - Mind Flay: now an explosion effect with no ND.
    - Punisher: timer reduction is more severe per skill point.

    - Rapture: now also increases cast rate; timer reduced per skill point, all the way to 0 timer; increased duration.

    - Plague: greatly increased damage. Did NOT replace the skill. Boo hoo.

    Sorceress

    - Ice Queen
    Ice Lance: increased freeze duration and missile speed.
    Frigid Sphere: increased damage.
    Ice Elementals: consolidated synergies, so you no longer need to max the entire cold tree; increased run speed; added +% defense aura (the other promised changes didn't work, sigh).

    - Stormfury
    Lightning Cascade: fixed desc error.
    Nova Charge: improved graphics.
    Warp Armor: avoid ramp is now slower, but linear.
    Warp Armor: corrected desc.

    - Sister
    Living Flame is a new level 6 skill, replacing Fear of Fire.
    Illumination: spell damage bonus is now linear.

    - Witch
    The poison tree is now more equal to the other trees:
    * Duration mostly reduced
    * Total damage reduced because of this
    * Damage per second left the same or boosted.
    * Now more spammable

    - Arcane Torrent: now has a mana cost; now does damage based on full mana.
    - Fixed huge unintended diminishing returns on Arcane Torrent and Mana Sweep.

    - Mystic Blood is a new level 90 skill, replacing Full Force.
    - Bladestorm moved up to level 24; fixed incorrectly high convert %.
    - Baneblade is a new level 90 skill.

    - Time Field: increased radius, is now again soft point based because Blizzard greatly disliked the concept of synergies on missile-carried curses.

    Other

    - Several skills added to the oskill list:
    Call Leprechaun, Death Ray, Deathstrike, Dominate, Elvensong, Exploding Totem, Fear Bomb Totem, Fire Bolt Nova, Holy Trap, Horned God [currently disabled], Overkill, Rune of Ice, Soulshatter, Spiral Dance, Summon Darklings, Whirlpool.
    - Also removed an oskill:
    Liche Totem (aura state cannibalised for druid melee tree).

    - The old 'melee druid oskills' (Feral Strike, Ravage, Thorn Field) now work with axes, maces and daggers, the same weapons as the shapeshifting trees.
    - Feral Strike: removed block bonus.

    top

    1.99d -> 1.A9 beta

    Characters

    - Base block modifier down to 0 for paladins, -1 for everyone else, -2 for sorcs.
    - Reduced mana per energy point by -1 (now you gain +2, +4 or +6) to reduce the chance of overflow with heavy investment.
    - Energy Factor power increased, but now tapers off at very high energy investments to prevent damage overflow.
    - The minion resistance cap is now +75%, up from 50% (and not 25%, liars).
    - Slightly reduced mana gain per energy point of some mana-intensive characters to avoid mana overflow.

    - All enemy-affecting resist pierce skills (except the assassin uberskill Phase Bomb) have been removed, leaving only item-based sources of -% resist (including Shadowfiends). This is because due to a bug in D2, they worked at full strength against immunities based on shield auras, making a lot of uberquests trivial to beat. Sorry, people.

    Amazon

    - Death Ray: fixed too-long formula causing erroneously low damage.
    - Dragonstrike replaces Wraith Arrow: fires a slow moving dragon that shoots spines at nearby enemies.
    - Ghost Arrow: added self-synergy for +1 arrow per 10 levels.
    - Fairy Ring: fixed base target seek range; +0.6 yards at all levels.
    - Moon Warrior: increased enhanced damage bonus from 15% to 20% per level.
    - Pact of Blood: duration now goes up with hard points.

    Assassin

    - Doom: reduced synergy from 20% to 15%.
    - Perfect Being: now based on hard points, but you get run speed from soft points.
    - Rocket Blade replaces Maelstrom: fires a zigzagging explosive knife.
    - Scorpion Blade: now gains +1 blade per 10 Broadside levels; synergy moved to Rocket Blade.
    - Singularity: mana cost frozen at 780.
    - Way of the Spider: poison length now increases by 0.2 seconds per level.

    Barbarian

    - Eagle Stance: heal rate now based on hard points, and there is now a slight damage penalty.
    - Kraken Stance: added max level synergy from all other stances.
    - Lion Stance: corrected display showing excessive damage; reduced ED% component; removed max level synergy but increased magic damage per level.
    - Predator replaces Berserk Fury: similar effect, but instead of hit recovery speed it offers life steal.
    - Runemaster: reduced by half.
    - Screaming Eagle replaces Eagle Dive: similar effect, but instead of resist pierce it reduces damage and attack speed.
    - Shower of Rocks: now instead of the (bugged) physical resist pierce, it reduces enemy damage. This is because the proposed -% attack rating change was useless because you didn't bother doing the math or you did and concluded that -50% attack rating is slightly inferior to x2 defense so it's weak and gimped. Please abandon your melee barb. I want you to make a bombsin.
    - Snake Stance: slowing effect is now a self-synergy.
    - Spirit Guide: now also adds +40% total defense, +15% per hard point.

    Necromancer

    - Buckshot: QUAD RANGE.
    - Deathstrike: doubled flat damage component, which isn't bugged.
    - Famine: reduced ED% to prevent damage overflow.
    - Fireheart Totem: to reduce lag, rate of fire divided by 4 but damage multipled by 4.
    - Necromantic Trance: added sound effect.
    - Summon Rampagor: poison damage now increases with character level, up to 5-10x higher than before!
    - Summon Void Archon: aura no longer reduces enemy resistance, but now reduces damage by 25%.

    Paladin

    - Edict of Forbiddance replaces Retribute: periodically deals weapon damage in an area.

    Sorceress

    - Fixes an issue where some lightning skills gained an incorrect bonus from energy factor.

    - Bladestorm: increased damage from 1/2 to 3/4.
    - Hive: synergy increased from 8% to 10%.
    - Nova Charge: synergy increased from 4% to 6%.
    - Spiral Dance replaces Starfire. Sorry to all Starfire users. See above. Also, the melee sorc's reliance on a single unique item sucked.
    - Time Field: no longer has ND.

    Patch 018 -> Patch 019

     

    Characters


    - People now start with the /players x pearl.
    - Rebalanced attribute gain.
    - Minion life generally reduced, but scales faster with character level.

    Amazon

    - All devotion skills are now level 18.

    - Barrage: halved arrow ramp.
    - Phalanx: doubled mana cost.
    - Trinity: clarified skill description; now has a self-synergy for increased damage.

    - Ricochet: changed graphic.
    - Fairy Ring: reduced base range and range per hard point.

    - Prowl: reduced poison length from 2 seconds to 1.6 seconds.
    - Lioness: skill level synergy now works correctly; NURFED DMG LOL.

    - Bloodlust: increased physical damage bonus.
    - Bacchanalia: tripled effect.
    - Bloodstorm: reduced self-synergy for extra bolts from ½ to ¼.

    - Blood Elementals: no longer requires a sceptre.
    - Pact of Blood: increased skill timer to 30 seconds; mana cost is now 0.

    - Blood Fury: toned down state lighting.

     

    Assassin

    - Batstrike: did something, I forgot what.
    - Crucify: added flat damage bonus per level; f this, I listened to whining again and buffed a skill that didn't need it again.
    - Hades Gate: slightly increased skill timer.

    - Wychwind: rift collision size 1 > 3.

    - Rain of Bombs: fixed damage display.

    Barbarian

    - Corrected spirit synergy descriptions.
    - Reverted Titan Strike icon, added new Earthquake icon by popular demand.

    - Blood Hatred: toned down state lighting; duration ramp is no longer erroneously 0.

    - Hawk Talons: reduced number of missiles at level 1.

    - Guard Tower: can now hit 0 timer at level 20, but reduced bonus duration.
    - Spirit Guide: reduced bonus from 15% to 10% per level.

    - Reduced spirit damage to prevent overflow.
    - Greater Manifestation: display is now correct.

    Druid

    - Rebalanced flat damage bonus on bow skills.

    - Hunting Banshee: increased synergy, then reduced it, then increased it. Whatever.
    - Fire Fountain: reduced number of fire spikes per level to fix lag issue.

    - Acid Fiends: now knows English.

    Necromancer

    - Totems now have a name when you target them.
    - Rearranged skill trees again.

    - Summon Darklings: thorns damage is now a flat bonus.
    - Summon Rampagor: doubled tainted blades damage.
    - Summon Lamia: reduced damage but added Doom effect.
    - Summon Void Archon: now 75% DR; greatly reduced damage but added AoE attack.

    - Sacrifices: now ignores shield auras; added 5 seconds to skill timer; +2 corpses at all levels.
    - Bend the Shadows: timer floor 0.2 seconds.

    - Death's Fury Totem: greatly reduced bonus, but now has a 50% (!) self-synergy.

    - Howling Totem: now correctly causes monster flee; increased crushing blow; added +dmg%.


    - Soulshatter: correctly affected by IAS and uses attack speed; LMB enabled; removed stun.

    - Buckshot: increased initial shards from 4 to 8.

    - Liche Form: description is now correct; slightly increased skill timer.

    Paladin

    - Arcane Strike: now does 3/2 damage for Plague purposes; reduced darkness effect.
    - Lemures: removed freeze effect.
    - Shadowfiends: Shadow Shroud buff duration increased to 10 seconds; added synergies.

    - Tainted Blood: now has the correct name on the LCS.
    - Dark King: reduced darkness effect.

    - Hymn: now has a graphic.

    - Scourge: increased damage synergy.

    Sorceress

    - Flamestrike: removed synergy.
    - Meteor Shower: increased mana cost.

    - Abyss: removed synergy.

    - Warp Armor: now adds avoidance instead of +hp%; defense bonus lowered.

    - Venomous Spirit: instead of a poison resist penalty, now has a cumulative speed penalty.
    - Hex: no longer costs 0.1 mana.

    Other skills

    - Blood Flash: description is now correct.
    - Bloodspeaker's Mark: it was 'too useless' on the zon, eh? It was 'bugged crap', eh?
    - Bloody Mary: now properly considered a buff skill.
    - Glacial Nova: no longer gains duration per level.

    - Pagan Heart: now properly considered a buff skill.
    - Spike Nova: now only hits once per target.
    - Touch of Death: toned down state lighting.
    - Yawn: there are no hidden messages in this changelog.
